                        match frame-type ethernet_II
                            dst-mac ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff
                            etype 0x8863
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 766 create
                        action accept
                        description "0x8863/PPPoE Discovery/----/Multicast"

                            dst-mac 01:00:5e:00:00:00 ff:ff:ff:80:00:00
                            etype 0x8863
                        exit
                    exit

                    exit

                cbs 50

                cbs 30

                exit
            exit

                queue 3
                egress-hsmda
                    queue 5
                exit
            exit
        exit

                start-avg 80
                max-avg 95
                max-prob 10
                no shutdown
            exit
            low-slope
                start-avg 30
                max-avg 95

            tier 1

                    rate 1002400
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit
